e_kuileitianzi = {
	color = { 96 3 42 }
	capital = c_wangcheng
	landless = yes

	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
	figurehead = yes
	allow_domicile = no
	always_follows_primary_heir = yes
	definite_form = yes
	can_create = {
		always = no
	}
	personal_relation_entry = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				exists = scope:target
				scope:liege ?= scope:target
			}
			desc = japan_personal_relation_ceremonial_liege_same
		}
			triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				exists = scope:liege
			}
			desc = japan_personal_relation_ceremonial_liege_other
		}

		}
	}
}
